# Evidence Expansion Pass — Chapters 13–28 — Pass 001

**Status:** Research remains open. This report audits the complete Evidence Improvement Queue universe for Chapters 13–28 under `PRODUCTION_EVIDENCE_POLICY.md` and the historical-evidence-review standard. It does not edit manuscript prose, claim maps, queues, Research records, architecture, or other upstream files.

## Executive Summary

- **Queue parity:** 366 of 366 listed claim IDs reported, in exact queue order, with no missing or extra IDs.
- **Recommendations:** KEEP 246; REWRITE 115; DEFER 5; REMOVE 0.
- **Citation strengthening:** Direct HTTP inspection verified the linked Gazette retrospectives used in Chapters 21 and 26; University of Iowa ArchivesSpace catalog pages for Milo Barta; institutional/corporate pages used in Chapter 22; and Internet Archive/Collins links used in Chapters 23–25. These checks improve traceability, not source rank.
- **New evidence:** No new primary source cleared a material person-level gate. The Barta catalog confirms a transcript exists but exposes no content. The Lindale retrospective remains secondary and supplies no Faulkes identity bridge, deed, transaction, capital, or authority chain.
- **Prose improvement:** REWRITE recommendations below bound moderate unhedged formulations to repository synthesis or inspected retrospective evidence. No manuscript changes were made.
- **Unresolved priorities:** (1) University of Iowa Barta transcript/audio and Wilson personnel/union records; (2) Linn County 1955–1960 grantor/grantee, mortgage, deed/option/lease records plus Faulkes identity and development-entity records; (3) transaction, authority, capital, chronology, labor, and consequence records named claim by claim.

## Method and Citation Audit

- Read the controlling queue, policy, all sixteen controlling claim maps, and all Chapter 13–28 Research records (using qualified v002 successors for Chapters 20 and 26).
- Preserved each controlling claim-map phrase and location verbatim. “Exact” therefore means exact controlling-map language; where a map records a repeated formulation rather than a full draft sentence, the map’s exact phrase is reproduced.
- Classified Research records as controlling synthesis, and Character Brief/NDR/Intent/Architecture as editorial controls rather than historical evidence. A catalog or title was never upgraded into content.
- Link audit: 15 directly cited endpoints returned HTTP 200, including Gazette, ArchivesSpace, Internet Archive, Grant Wood/UIowa, Cedar Rapids, Emil Frei, and Collins Story pages. Two Iowa Digital Library nodes returned HTTP 403 and remain inaccessible leads. Search/extract provider calls returned HTTP 432; direct HTTP inspection was used instead.
- Directly inspected the Barta transcript catalog page: it confirms “Barta, Milo — Transcript,” November 30, 1977, ILHOP MsZ71, University of Iowa Special Collections, and “No requestable containers.” It does not reveal testimony.
- Directly inspected the Gazette Lindale article text. It reports the 1956 announcement, Faulkes/Thompson site association, local opposition, Greenbaum construction, and 1960 opening. It does not identify Faulkes, state the land instrument, or allocate capital/authority.
- Directly inspected the Gazette Snyder article text, confirming its retrospective statements for startup, Jordan co-agency, office, depot routine, destinations, mileage, retirement, and continuity. It remains retrospective secondary evidence.

## Closing Findings

- **Strengthened citations:** Direct page access and text inspection strengthened traceability for Snyder/Mari-An, Lindale, Barta catalog existence, Grant Wood project sources, and Collins materials. No direct check justified upgrading a secondary or catalog source to primary evidence.
- **New evidence:** The Barta transcript catalog’s exact citation and access condition were confirmed; this narrows the retrieval intervention but does not establish risk. The Lindale article was re-inspected and preserves divided agency; it adds no Faulkes identity/authority/capital proof.
- **Prose improvements:** Claims marked REWRITE should be attributed to repository synthesis or the inspected retrospective until the named record is obtained. KEEP preserves already bounded prose and negative-evidence statements. DEFER withholds low-confidence detail rather than laundering it through repetition.
- **Research remains open:** Priority retrieval is the Barta transcript/audio and Wilson records, followed by Linn County Faulkes/Thompson land and mortgage instruments, identity bridges, development-entity filings, financing, contracts, and anchor leases.
